Source Code

This is the source-code for the Apollo 9 Command Module's Guidance Computer. These files were derived originally from the scan from MIT's Dibner Institute's now-discontinued website titled "History of Recent Science and Technology", which in turn was originally created by Gary Neff, though his high-quality scans were unfortunately reduced in legibility when presented online. The markings on the front of the printout imply that it was the original AGC developer Norm Brodeur's copy. A scan by Ron Burkey has superceded it, made from a more-legible copy from the collection of original AGC developer Fred Martin. The source code was transcribed from those images by Ron Burkey. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	ASSEMBLE REVISION 249 OF AGC PROGRAM COLOSSUS BY NASA 2021111-041
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

001536,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     Part of the source code for Colossus, build 249.
001537,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Command Module's (CM)
001538,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), for Apollo 9.
001539,000007:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001540,000008:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 35-126.

001547,000015:                                                                                                  ##                              was working is that INTVEC isn't used for 
001548,000016:                                                                                                  ##                              anything.

Page 35 

001594,000062:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001595,000063: 
001596,000064:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001597,000065:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001598,000066:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001599,000067: 
001600,000068:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  START
001601,000069:                                                                                                  #                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001602,000070:                                                                                                  #                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001603,000071: 
001604,000072:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001605,000073:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001606,000074:                                                                                                  #                USUALLY NUMERIC, IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.                 )
001607,000075: 
001608,000076:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001609,000077:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001610,000078: 
001611,000079:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  Y
001612,000080: 
001613,000081:                                                                                                  #        =       MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001614,000082:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001615,000083: 
001616,000084:                                                                                                  #                        X       =       Y
001617,000085: 
001618,000086:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001619,000087:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM. M(SIZE)N.
001620,000088: 
001621,000089:                                                                                                  #                M       REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001622,000090:                                                                                                  #                        B       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001623,000091:                                                                                                  #                                INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001624,000092:                                                                                                  #                        I       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001625,000093:                                                                                                  #                                INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001626,000094:                                                                                                  #                                INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001627,000095: 
001628,000096:                                                                                                  #                SIZE    IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001629,000097: 
001630,000098:                                                                                                  #                N       INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001631,000099:                                                                                                  #                        PL      MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001632,000100:                                                                                                  #                        DSP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001633,000101:                                                                                                  #                        PRM     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT,  IE. IT
001634,000102:                                                                                                  #                                IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001635,000103:                                                                                                  #                                PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001636,000104:                                                                                                  #                        TMP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001637,000105:                                                                                                  #                                IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001638,000106:                                                                                                  #                                IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001639,000107:                                                                                                  #                                PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001640,000108:                                                                                                  #                                CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 36 

001642,000110:                                                                                                  #                                IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001643,000111:                                                                                                  #                                IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001644,000112:                                                                                                  #                        IN      MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001645,000113:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001646,000114:                                                                                                  #                        OUT     MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001647,000115:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001648,000116:

001650,000118:                                                                                                  #  SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001651,000119: 
001652,000120: 37,2001                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001653,000121: 37,2001                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001654,000122: 37,2001                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001655,000123: 37,2001                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001656,000124: 37,2001                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001657,000125: 37,2001                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001658,000126: 37,2001                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001659,000127:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001660,000128: 
001661,000129: 37,2001                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001662,000130: 37,2001                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001663,000131: 37,2001                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001664,000132: 37,2001                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001665,000133: 37,2001                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001666,000134: 37,2001                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001667,000135: 37,2001                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.
001668,000136: 
001669,000137: 37,2001                        CYR                EQUALS   20                                    
001670,000138: 37,2001                        SR                 EQUALS   21                                    
001671,000139: 37,2001                        CYL                EQUALS   22                                    
001672,000140: 37,2001                        EDOP               EQUALS   23                                    #  EDITS INTERPRETIVE OPERATION CODE PAIRS.
001673,000141: 
001674,000142: 37,2001                        TIME2              EQUALS   24                                    
001675,000143: 37,2001                        TIME1              EQUALS   25                                    
001676,000144: 37,2001                        TIME3              EQUALS   26                                    
001677,000145: 37,2001                        TIME4              EQUALS   27                                    
001678,000146: 37,2001                        TIME5              EQUALS   30                                    
001679,000147: 37,2001                        TIME6              EQUALS   31                                    
001680,000148: 37,2001                        CDUX               EQUALS   32                                    
001681,000149: 37,2001                        CDUY               EQUALS   33                                    
001682,000150: 37,2001                        CDUZ               EQUALS   34                                    
001683,000151: 37,2001                        CDUT               EQUALS   35                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION CDU (WAS OPTY).
001684,000152: 37,2001  0000035               OPTY               =        CDUT                                  
001685,000153: 37,2001                        CDUS               EQUALS   36                                    #  OPTICS SHAFT CDU (WAS OPTX).
001686,000154: 37,2001  0000036               OPTX               =        CDUS                                  
001687,000155: 37,2001                        PIPAX              EQUALS   37                                    
001688,000156: 37,2001                        PIPAY              EQUALS   40                                    
001689,000157: 37,2001                        PIPAZ              EQUALS   41                                    
001690,000158: 37,2001                        BMAGX              EQUALS   42                                    
001691,000159: 37,2001                        BMAGY              EQUALS   43                                    
001692,000160: 37,2001                        BMAGZ              EQUALS   44                                    
001693,000161: 37,2001                        INLINK             EQUALS   45                                    
001694,000162: 37,2001                        RNRAD              EQUALS   46                                    
001695,000163: 37,2001                        GYROCTR            EQUALS   47                                    
001696,000164: 37,2001                        GYROCMD            EQUALS   47                                    
001697,000165: 37,2001                        CDUXCMD            EQUALS   50                                    
001698,000166: 37,2001                        CDUYCMD            EQUALS   51

001702,000170: 37,2001  0000053               OPTYCMD            =        CDUTCMD                               
001703,000171: 37,2001  0000053               TVCYAW             EQUALS   CDUTCMD                               #  SPS YAW COMMAND IN TVC MODE.

001707,000175: 37,2001                        EMSD               EQUALS   55

001718,000186: 37,2001                        X2                 EQUALS   39D                                   #  TO THE WORK AREA.

002989,001457:                                                                                                  #  (ITEMP1 THROUGH RUPTREG4)             
002990,001458: 
002991,001459:                                                                                                  #  ANY OF THESE MAY BE USED AS TEMPORARIES DURING INTERRUPT OR WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED. THE ITEMP SERIES
002992,001460:                                                                                                  #  IS USED DURING CALLS TO THE EXECUTIVE AND WAITLIST - THE RUPTREGS ARE NOT.

002996,001464:    0062     0061               EXECTEM1           EQUALS   ITEMP1

003039,001507: 
003040,001508:                                                                                                  #  EXEC TEMPORARIES WHICH MAY BE USED BETWEEN CCS NEWJOBS.
003041,001509:                                                                                                  #  (INTB15+ THROUGH RUPTMXM)             (32D)
003042,001510:    0114                        INTB15+            ERASE                                          #  REFLECTS 15TH BIT OF INDEXABLE ADDRESSES
003043,001511:    0115     0114               DSEXIT             EQUALS   INTB15+                               #  RETURN FOR DSPIN
003044,001512:    0115     0114               EXITEM             EQUALS   INTB15+                               #  RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT

003046,001514: 
003047,001515:    0115                        INTBIT15           ERASE                                          #  SIMILAR TO ABOVE.
003048,001516:    0116     0115               WRDRET             EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  RETURN FOR 5BLANK
003049,001517:    0116     0115               WDRET              EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  RETURN FOR DSPWD
003050,001518:    0116     0115               DECRET             EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
003051,001519:    0116     0115               21/22REG           EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  TEMP FOR CHARIN
003052,001520: 
003053,001521:                                                                                                  #  THE REGISTERS BETWEEN ADDRWD AND PRIORITY MUST STAY IN THE FOLLOWING ORDER FOR INTERPRETIVE TRACE.
